1093        <!-- Shortcuts Samples -->
1094
1095
1096        <!-- This section of sample code shows how your application can add shortcuts to -->
1097        <!-- the launcher (home screen).  Shortcuts have a three step life cycle. -->
1098
1099
1100        <!-- 1.  Your application offers to provide shortcuts to the launcher.  When -->
1101        <!-- the user installs a shortcut, an activity within your application -->
1102        <!-- generates the actual shortcut and returns it to the launcher, where it -->
1103        <!-- is shown to the user as an icon. -->
1104
1105
1106        <!-- 2.  Any time the user clicks on an installed shortcut, an intent is sent. -->
1107        <!-- Typically this would then be handled as necessary by an activity within -->
1108        <!-- your application. -->
1109
1110
1111        <!-- 3.  The shortcut is deleted.  There is no notification to your application. -->
1112
1113
1114        <!-- In order provide shortcuts from your application, you provide three things: -->
1115
1116
1117        <!-- 1.  An intent-filter declaring your ability to provide shortcuts -->
1118        <!-- 2.  Code within the activity to provide the shortcuts as requested -->
1119        <!-- 3.  Code elsewhere within your activity, if appropriate, to receive -->
1120        <!-- intents from the shortcut itself. -->
1121
